  <div class="max-width-2 mx-auto px2">
    <div class="clearfix pb4">
      <p class="m-lessoncontent-desc-body"></p><p>Use your newfound JavaScript skills to challenge your friends and family in a game of hangman.</p><p></p>
      <article class="m-lessoncontent" data-lesson-id="14107">
        <h1>Wordgame - Take Two</h1>
<h2>Take Two Instructions</h2>
<p>In your existing hangman repo:</p>

<ul>
<li>Tag your current version as version 0.1.0:<br>
<code>git tag --annotate v0.1.0 -m "original attempt"</code>
</li>
<li>Push your tagged version up to github:<br>
<code>git push origin --tags</code>
</li>
<li>Make a new git branch named "take-tdd":<br>
<code>git checkout -b "take-tdd"</code>
</li>
<li>If you haven't already done so, make the "master" branch the active github-pages branch.</li>
<li>
<em>Using TDD and the published testing framework of your choice</em>, finish your previous hangman assignment, ensuring:

<ul>
<li>that you push your "take-tdd" branch up to GitHub regularly</li>
<li>that when you have a new feature implemented, you merge the current 
"take-tdd" branch into your "master" branch and push it up to GitHub</li>
<li>that your "master" branch never loses a feature it already had (i.e. always leave it better than you found it!)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>When you submit your assignment, ensure that:

<ul>
<li>the github repo is your officially submitted url (e.g. "<a href="https://github.com/user-name/proj-name%22" target="_blank">https://github.com/user-name/proj-name"</a>)</li>
<li>you include <em>both</em>

<ul>
<li>the github-pages link (e.g. "<a href="https://user-name.github.io/proj-name%22" target="_blank">https://user-name.github.io/proj-name"</a>)</li>
<li>a link to your test file/directory in the github repo (e.g. "<a href="https://github.com/user-name/proj-name/tree/master/test/feat-tape.test.js%22" target="_blank">https://github.com/user-name/proj-name/tree/master/test/feat-tape.test.js"</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2>Description</h2>
<p>You know the word-guessing game hangman? Well that's what you'll be building with this assignment.</p>
<p>Basically, it works like this:</p>

<ul>
<li>The app starts by choosing a random word</li>
<li>The player can guess a single letter at a time</li>
<li>The player has a fixed number of turns in which to guess all of the letters in the word</li>
<li>The app should indicate when the player has won or lost</li>
</ul>
<p>You can get super fancy with it... e.g. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TE9ahmj_5Hc" target="_blank">Hangman Hero Android App demo</a>.</p>
<h2>Objectives</h2>
<p>You should…</p>

<ul>
<li>Demonstrate correct use of functions, conditionals, loops, arrays</li>
<li>Properly sequence JavaScript statements</li>
<li>Change the DOM based on application state (win/loss, valid/invalid guess)</li>
</ul>
<h2>Details</h2>
<h3>Instructions</h3>

<ul>
<li>Create your project</li>
<li>Create a file called for your words (e.g <code>js/common-words.js</code>) and paste this into it:</li>
</ul>
<pre class="highlight javascript"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code><span class="c1">// Here are the 100 most popular words in English, as totally</span>
<span class="c1">// stolen from here: https://gist.github.com/gravitymonkey/2406023</span>
<span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">commonWords</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span>
  <span class="s2">"the"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"of"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"and"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"a"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"to"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"in"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"is"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"you"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"that"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"it"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"he"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"was"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"for"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"on"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"are"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"as"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"with"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"his"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"they"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"I"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"at"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"be"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"this"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"have"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"from"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"or"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"one"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"had"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"by"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"word"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"but"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"not"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"what"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"all"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"were"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"we"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"when"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"your"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"can"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"said"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"there"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"use"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"an"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"each"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"which"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"she"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"do"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"how"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"their"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"if"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"will"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"up"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"other"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"about"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"out"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"many"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"then"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"them"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"these"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"so"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"some"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"her"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"would"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"make"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"like"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"him"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"into"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"time"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"has"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"look"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"two"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"more"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"write"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"go"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"see"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"number"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"no"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"way"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"could"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"people"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"my"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"than"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"first"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"water"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"been"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"call"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"who"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"oil"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"its"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"now"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"find"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"long"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"down"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"day"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"did"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"get"</span><span class="p">,</span>
  <span class="s2">"come"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"made"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"may"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"part"</span>
<span class="p">];</span>
</code></pre>
<h3>Example</h3>
<p>Say your game logic has chosen the word: "hello".</p>
<p>You should display:</p>
<pre class="highlight plaintext"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code>_ _ _ _ _
</code></pre>
<p>A visual indication (such as an underscore) for each letter in the word.</p>
<p>You should also display the number of turns remaining:</p>
<pre class="highlight plaintext"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code>Turns: 8
</code></pre>
<p>Next, the user guesses: a</p>
<p>You should decrement the number of turns remaining:</p>
<pre class="highlight plaintext"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code>Turns: 7 
</code></pre>
<p>And also continue displaying:</p>
<pre class="highlight plaintext"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code>_ _ _ _ _
</code></pre>
<p>Next, the user guesses: l</p>
<p>You should display:</p>
<pre class="highlight plaintext"><span class="highlight-copy-clipboard hint--left hint--rounded hint--no-animate" data-hint="Copy Code"></span><code>Turns: 7 

_ _ l l _
</code></pre>
<p>And so forth.</p>
<h3>Deliverables</h3>

<ul>
<li>The GitHub Repo url, containing:

<ul>
<li>standard repository files</li>
<li><code>index.html</code></li>
<li>A file with just your words list.  All words must be longer than 2 characters.</li>
<li>One or more CSS files in their own sub-directory</li>
<li>One or more JavaScript files in their own sub-directory</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The GitHub pages url</li>
</ul>
<h2>Apprehensive Apprentice</h2>
<p>The game should:</p>

<ul>
<li>Choose a random word <em>of 3 letters or more</em> from your words list.</li>
<li>Allow the user to guess one letter at a time.</li>
<li>When the user runs out of turns, show a losing screen.</li>
<li>When the user guesses all of the letters in the word, show a winning screen.</li>
<li>May use any non-console mechanism to interact with the user (e.g. 
prompt and alert are acceptable, as are input and manipulating DOM 
elements, but console.log and setting the current letter from the 
browser's console are not).</li>
</ul>
<h2>Skilled Sorcerer</h2>
<p>Apprehensive Apprentice mode plus the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>Don't let the user guess the same letter more than once.</li>
<li>Display all guesses on the user's screen so the user knows what letters he/she has already guessed.</li>
<li>Must use an HTML5 interface to get user inputs and display information to the user (i.e. may <em>not</em> use prompt and alerts).</li>
<li>Make it look good! Instead of showing the number of turns, you could show a health meter or <a href="http://i.stack.imgur.com/iMqfw.jpg" target="_blank">ascii art</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Wise Wizard</h2>
<p>Skilled Sorcerer mode plus any or all of the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>Make it look amazing by showing an animation of the body part swaying when the user guesses incorrectly (you <em>may</em> want to start with a <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/SVG/Tutorial/Basic_Shapes" target="_blank">basic SVG</a> line and circle and then add the appropriate css transition or <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=f1WMjDx4snI" target="_blank">animation</a>.</li>
<li>Make it sound great by playing a <a href="https://duckduckgo.com/?q=death+dirge" target="_blank">death dirge</a> or other such audio when the user guesses incorrectly.</li>
<li>When the player loses, play a video or show some funny losing animation.</li>
</ul>
      </article>
    </div>
  </div>

          <div class="l-navigator-drawer-unit-title" title="Scrappy Hour" data-navigator-toggleunit="">
